< Review>
I'm the pickiest person I know when it comes to getting my nails done, but I'm also completely happy to pay and tip well for a top notch experience.  I want a strong massage and will usually order an extra 10-20 minutes, depending on my week so far.  I want service verging on spoiling, and I don't mind having a conversation with my nail technician but I HATE when they speak Vietnamese to each other and laugh while I'm wondering if it's about me.  Once they see that I'm in the "zone", I want to be able to sink into my chair and drift off.

I get ALL OF THIS at Nails & Spa... and more.  They recognize me, call me by name, always provide a cold water bottle, and they are genuinely NICE people.  They have a million gel choices, a great selection of polishes, and I get a monthly wax (I won't admit it, though) and NEVER have red blotchy marks on my face.  I rarely have the ability to make an appointment, but they always seem able to accommodate.

Of all the places I've gone, this is the one I keep returning to because they are kind, considerate and CONSISTENT.  There are 2 nail places in this center, so make sure you're at the one right next to the tattoo shop!!</Review>

< text>
If you only get the garlic mushrooms Skosh Monahan's is worth going to but I warn you, come with an appetite and if you order the garlic mushrooms, share them. They are tender, juicy, seasoned just right and there are a lot of them! Served with fresh sliced French or Italian bread they are a meal in themselves!

The ribeye steak would have been really good if it was a slightly better cut of well marbled meat. As it was the seasoning was fine and it was definitely more than just edible. The vegetables however, gave new meaning to the word "al dente." Cooking them for another 30 seconds to a minute would have made them perfect. As with everything else, there were plenty of them.

The service was excellent and cordial. The atmosphere was a bit more subdued than your typical Sports Bar which I considered good. I don't like to be deafened while I eat. Prices won't bankrupt you but I wouldn't rate them on the low end of moderate either.

All in all, this place is definitely worth a visit if you are anywhere nearby.<//text>

<userid>101068692969669901262< /userid>< text>
Great theater, and super big for it's location, and age. For those of you complaining of the bathroom smell... the bathroom features 2 urinals, and a single stall. Unlike Regal Cinema, or massive theaters... the toilets are all right next to each other, and cannot be properly ventilated. So it will smell like bathroom. And the staff consists of excellently chosen, well behaved people, but they are always short staffed, and clean the best they can between showings... sometimes they miss stuff. But the place is always clean. If it isn't, don't complain on here. Or whine. Please inform the employees so they can fix it. Don't be the problem, be the solution. :D</text>

The owner of Angels Theatre, Jeff, has done wonders to restore this lovely old theater. What's more, he is truly happy to share his knowledge and love of film. <review>LOVE this theatre!! This is the first theatre that I ever went to as a child- saw "M*A*S*H" with my folks way back when (my mom threw her sweater over my head at the juicy parts....). This is the theatre where my own family spent so many happy hours. Efficient, fun and quirky staff, comfy new seats, good sound and clarity, kitschy Gold Rush/western themed murals, good popcorn-what else could you want?! < review>
TLDR: Excellent prices, excellent service, professional work. This is the place to go for any tire related anything, and is now my personal go-to for tires that I would recommend to everyone.

Full review:

I have been to several tire places and this one is the best of the lot without question.

I called ahead to make sure they had what I needed, as the vehicle in question has uncommon tires. There was a short wait while stock was confirmed, and was subsequently pleasantly suprised to hear the not only did they have 4 tires of the correct size, but they were able to undercut their competitions price.

There is no reduction of quality of service and work from the lower price, which is a definite win in my book. It did take longer than one might expect, but that was due to my tires being really wide as well as run-flat tires, which adds a significant degree of difficulty (have done tires myself in the past with a manual tire machine, so have a bit of experience in this area). Despite the difficulty,  the work was done with no complaints and the team of two brothers worked together very well to complete the job to perfection. They realised that the work was taking a while without me saying anything, and proceeded to explain exactly what was going on without any prompting at all, which shows their professionalism and knowledge in action.

After all was said and done, I was told to bring my car right back if there were any issues and they would take care of it. These guys rock!

2 Months Later: As happy now as on day 1; my truck needs tires soon and I know exactly who to call!

7 Months Later: Awesomely epic service, 'nuff said</review>

< review>
2-star specifically for non-members/non-resident activity pool. Went here today for the first time with the wife, the grandparents, and two kids (2 and 4.5) for the 12:30-2:30 session. Now, once we got in we had an absolute blast, but the 2-star review is due to our awful experience before we entered the pool area (considered 1-star but wanted to factor in that we did have a fun time in the water). NON-MEMBERS: BE ADVISED. LONG LINE WAITS. Not to be dramatic, but at one point while we were waiting in line it was so bad my 4.5 year old started crying and said, "Dad, can we please just leave and go to the water front park?" (And it wasn't a typical 4-year-old bratty/whining cry. It was a genuine sad/disappointed cry.) Basically what happened was, we got there at Noon and were close to the front of the "Non-member" line, but we didn't get in to the actual pool area until 1pm, and that was only because at 12:50 (20 minutes after the the session opened) I went up to the lifeguard who was processing everyone (members) in and asked her when they were going to start to also process the non-members. She said that she was going to process all of the members first before she started the non-members (which at the rate things were going and how many members there still were in line we MAYBE would have gotten into the pool at 1:30.) So I asked her to double check with a supervisor on their policy (because if that were the case we would've left.) Thankfully she checked because when she came back they started processing the non-members as well. All that to say, it was a very stressful and very disappointing way to start off what (thankfully) ended up being a fun afternoon at the pool. And although it ended up being fun, unless they change their process or non-member/resident price, I don't plan on going back. It's just not worth it for price, wait in line, and limited time alowed inside. I get that members/residents have priority, but still..it doesn't need to be this bad. (Maybe process people who are in line early and have a separate staging area where people who are already processed can wait and then go right in when the session starts?) Last comment...I feel like most of the disappointment could've been avoided if they communicated better and put on their website "non-member spots limited. Arrive early. Expect long waits. Cost is for one 2-hour session only" Unless I missed it, nowhere did the website communicate any of that. Please let me know if you improve the non-member check in process! Would love to come back if you do!<//review>

<rate>1</rate>< review>
I'm only giving 1 star for this reason....
It was our first time swimming here and I let the girl who checked us in know that. However, she never informed me that there were timed sessions and everyone must exit and pay again to re-enter.
My kids live in Santee but I live in San Diego so I had to pay non resident price of $16 for the 2 of them (otherwise it should have been $3 each).... 45 minutes after being there, (at about 1:10pm) they find a turd in the children's pool. The whole staff comes running out screaming "the pool is closed" so everyone starts leaving. They said the pool would re-open at 2pm and that we needed to exit and wait in line to get back in and pay ANOTHER $16!!!!
Needless to say we won't be returning to the YMCA<//review>
